============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK17)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_f*A**c3
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function
\[
F(t,A)=0.2084703204063362\,A^{1/3}\;-\;0.6750544468008356\,A\,e^{-0.0783132263146032\,t}.
\]
So any matching candidate must be able to represent **exactly** “(constant)\(\cdot A^{1/3}\) + (constant)\(\cdot A\exp(k t)\)” with **no extra dependence** on \(t\) or \(A\) (beyond those two terms), for all real \(t,A\).

---

### 1. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 \max(0,c4+t)\)
To equal GT for all \(t\), the \(\max(0,c4+t)\) term must vanish identically. Only way: set \(c3=0\). Then it reduces to candidate 2 form, which can match (see 2).  
**Match possible** (via \(c3=0\)).

### 2. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t}\)
This has exactly the same structure as GT. Choose:
- \(c0 = 0.2084703204063362\)
- \(c1 = -0.6750544468008356\)
- \(c2 = -0.0783132263146032\)
Then candidate equals GT for all \(t,A\).  
**Match possible**.

### 3. Candidate 2 + \(A c3\max(0,c4+t) + A c5/(A+c6)\)
Need both extra terms to be identically zero for all \(t,A\).
- Set \(c3=0\) kills the Max term.
- For \(A c5/(A+c6)\) to be identically 0 for all \(A\), must set \(c5=0\).
Then reduces to candidate 2, which matches.  
**Match possible**.

### 4. Candidate 2 + \(A c3\max(0,c4+t) + c5 e^{c6 t}\max(0,c7+t)\)
Kill extras: set \(c3=0\) and \(c5=0\). Reduces to candidate 2.  
**Match possible**.

### 5. Candidate 2 + \(A c3\max(0,c4+t) + A c5/(A+c6) + c7\)
Need constant offset \(c7\) to be 0, and the two extra terms to vanish: set \(c3=0, c5=0, c7=0\). Reduces to candidate 2.  
**Match possible**.

### 6. Candidate 2 + \(A c3\max(0,c4+t) + c5 e^{c6 t}\log(c7|A|+1)\)
To match GT (which has no log term), must set \(c5=0\). Also set \(c3=0\). Reduces to candidate 2.  
**Match possible**.

---

From here on, check whether the candidate can be reduced (by setting parameters to 0) to exactly the two-term GT form. If a candidate cannot produce an \(A^{1/3}\) term at all, it cannot match.

### 7. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + \dots + c7 e^{c8 e^{c9 t}}\)
No \(A^{1/3}\) term exists anywhere. Even if many terms are zeroed, remaining terms are \(A e^{c1 t}\) plus possibly constants in \(t\). Cannot create \(A^{1/3}\).  
**No match**.

### 8. Rational-in-\(A\) terms with \((A+c4)\) denominators and cosines
No \(A^{1/3}\) term. Also has unavoidable rational structure unless coefficients set to 0, but then you lose needed terms.  
**No match**.

### 9. \(A^{c0}c1 e^{A c2} + c3 t^{c4} + c5 + c6 e^{c7 t}\log(A c8+1)\)
Has \(e^{A c2}\) (wrong dependence on \(A\)) unless \(c2=0\), but then first term becomes \(c1 A^{c0}\) (could make \(A^{1/3}\)). However GT also needs \(-0.675 A e^{kt}\), and there is no \(A e^{kt}\) term available (the log term is wrong form).  
**No match**.

### 10. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + \dots + A^{c6}c7/(A^{c6}+c8)+\dots\)
No \(A^{1/3}\) term; only \(A\) times exponential plus rational forms.  
**No match**.

### 11. \(\frac{A c0}{A c1+1} + \frac{A c2 e^{c3 t}}{A c1+1} + A c4 + \frac{c5 e^{c3 t}}{A c1+1}\)
No \(A^{1/3}\). Denominators prevent matching pure \(A^{1/3}\) term; setting \(c1=0\) removes denominator but still only linear in \(A\) plus constant/exponential terms, not \(A^{1/3}\).  
**No match**.

### 12–13. Include \(A e^{c1 t}\) plus rational/sqrt/cos terms
No \(A^{1/3}\) term.  
**No match** for 12, 13.

### 14–17. Polynomial/sqrt/rational/tanh/exp(A⋅) mixtures
None contain \(A^{1/3}\) as a free power term (they have \(A^2\), \(A\), or \(A^{c}\) but coupled with other structures not removable to exactly \(A^{1/3}\) + \(A e^{kt}\) while keeping both required terms). In particular:
- 14 has \(A^{c1}c2 e^{c3 t}\) but also \(A^2 c0\) and \(e^{A c8}\); you can zero extra terms, but then you still lack a standalone \(A^{1/3}\) term unless you set \(c1=1/3\) and remove \(t\)-dependence by \(c3=0\), but then you lose the needed \(A e^{kt}\) term (only one such exponential-in-\(t\) term exists).
- 15–17 similarly have only linear-in-\(A\) and rational/sqrt pieces; no \(A^{1/3}\).
**No match** for 14–17.

### 18. \(A^{c0}c1 e^{c2 t} + c3 e^{c4/(c5+t)} + c6\log(c7 e^{c8 t}+1)\)
Could make \(A^{1/3}\) by \(c0=1/3\) and \(c2=0\), but then no \(A e^{kt}\) term. If instead make \(c0=1\) to get \(A e^{kt}\), then no \(A^{1/3}\) term. Only one \(A^{c0}\) term exists, so cannot get both required \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A e^{kt}\) simultaneously.  
**No match**.

### 19. All terms are rational with denominator \(A+c1\) and exponentials in \(1/(c8+t)\)
No \(A^{1/3}\) term and wrong \(t\)-dependence.  
**No match**.

### 20. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2/(A c3+1)^2 + A c4/(A+c5) + A c6 + c7 t + c8\)
No \(A^{1/3}\).  
**No match**.

### 21. \(A^{c0}c1 e^{c2 t} + A^{c3}c4 e^{c5/(c6+t)} + c7 e^{c8/(c9+t)}\)
Has two power terms in \(A\), but the second has \(e^{c5/(c6+t)}\) (wrong \(t\)-dependence) unless you kill it. If you kill it, you only have one \(A^{c0}\) term, so cannot get both \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A e^{kt}\).  
**No match**.

### 22. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + c2\tanh(\cdot)+ c5 e^{A c6}+ c7\log(A c8+1)\)
No \(A^{1/3}\).  
**No match**.

### 23. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A^{c2}c3 + c4 e^{c1 t} + c5 t/(c6+t)\)
This *can* represent both needed terms:
- Set \(c2=1/3\) and \(c3=0.2084703204063362\) to get \(0.20847 A^{1/3}\).
- Set \(c0=-0.6750544468008356\), \(c1=-0.0783132263146032\) to get \(-0.67505 A e^{-0.0783 t}\).
- Kill extra terms: set \(c4=0\) and \(c5=0\).
Then exactly equals GT.  
**Match possible**.

### 24. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 + A c2 e^{c3 t^{c4}} + A c5 + c6\)
No \(A^{1/3}\).  
**No match**.

### 25. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2/(A c3+1)^2 + A c4/(c5+t)^{0.5} + A c6/(A c7+1)^2 + c8\)
No \(A^{1/3}\).  
**No match**.

### 26–27. No \(A^{1/3}\) term (contain exp(A⋅), logs, tanh)
**No match**.

### 28. Many terms all divided by \(c2+t\)
GT has no such denominator; cannot remove it for all \(t\) (no parameter choice makes \(1/(c2+t)\equiv 1\)).  
**No match**.

### 29–30. \(A c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t^{c3}} + A c4/(A+c5) + c6\) (or \(A c4/(A c5+1)\))
No \(A^{1/3}\).  
**No match**.

### 31,35,40. Tanh terms with denominators; no \(A^{1/3}\)
**No match**.

### 32–34,36–39,41–50 (remaining)
All fail because they either:
- lack any \(A^{1/3}\) term entirely, or
- cannot simultaneously produce both \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A e^{kt}\) without introducing non-removable extra \(t\)- or \(A\)-dependence (denominators in \(t\), logs, tanh, exp(A⋅), etc.).
